-04- COMMANDS
------------------------------------------------------------

BioFire
-------
Use the combo Bio Blast + Fire.

BolLago
-------
Use the combo Bolt 3 + Lagomorph.

Cycloni
-------
Use the skill 'Cyclonic'

H-Bomb
-------
Use the skill 'H-Bomb'

Overcas
-------
Use the skill 'Overcast'

R-Heal
-------
Use a random HP- and/or MP-restoring skill.
Equal chance of any of the following:
  Cure, Cure 2, Cure 3, Heal Force, Ice Rabbit, Life, Life 2, Mantra, Pearl Wind, Phoenix, Spiraler, Sraphim, Starlet, Sun Bath, Tapir, Wild Bear

R-Nuke
-------
Use a random non-elemental magic damage skill.
Equal chance of any of the following:
  7-Flush, Bahamut, Blow Fish, Bum Rush, Cokatrice, Crusader, Drain, Empowerer, Exploder, Flare, Flash, Goner, H-Bomb, Heart Burn, HyperDrive, L.4 Flare, Land Slide, Maduin, Megahit, Meteo, Meteor, Osmose, Rage, Rasp, Retort, Revenge, Shrapnel, Step Mine, Stone, Stunner, Ultima, Whump

Slow2
-------
Use the skill 'Slow 2'

6. R, Y, right, right, down-right, down, down-left, left
7. Y, right, left, up-left, up, up-right, right
8. right, up-right, up, down, X, left, up-left, up, down, R
